=== [2025-11-30] simple-games ===
Before we get to snake, lets take a step back and enhance hot potato

My daughter recommended that instead of just hitting a pass button we change up the UI for multi player. We instead have an internal countdown, 10s to 30s, instead of a random pass count. if you have the potato on your device it appears in the middle of a circle. There are N-1 (where N is the number of players in the game, that is Host + clients) boxes on the parimeter of the box (equal spaced) and the player with the potato has to drag it to one of these boxes. the boxes represent other players in the game and it sends the potato to that player and it appears on that players device now. I would like to have each box be a random unnamed player, and each pass it's scrambled for each device. that way you can't know who your passing it to, and if you keep dragging it to the same box it wont go to the same person each time.

=== [2025-11-30] simple-games ===
Add another to the list, a taco/cat/goat/cheese/pizza, not something that'll work single player really (we can still have it, but it'd be more like practice)

the idea of taco/cat/goat/cheese pizza, is that each person turns over a card and lays it onto the stack, it starts with Taco, if they turn over any card except taco, nothing happens, if the card lines up, and they turn over what they said, then everyone races to slap the deck (or in this case touch the phone screen) the last person to touch the phone screen looses and tacks the discard pile.

we could do a variation on that game, there are 3 special action cards, like narwall (you have to slap your hands above your head first, here we could drag up from the bottom of the screen) or goundhog (you have to slap the table, here we could drag down), then gorilla, you have to pound your chest 3 times, here we could have you alternatingly tap two icons back and forth 3 times.

Lets create a new document MULTIPLAYER_FIXES.md and put in there code analysis and proper play order plans for tournament style (single elemenation) tic-tac-toe and connect 4. read our plans in N_PLAYER_PLAN.md and the code to get a sense of what's going on. Write up the flow of the code and possible places where player rotation order isn't being handled. come up with steps to resolve those issues and have a game play rotation that's described here:

for tournament play:
pick random groups of 2 players and have them battle.
if there is an odd number of players as soon as one of the games resolve have them play the winner if anyone is just in the lobby and it's their turn to play, put them into their game switching to active game screen. Always have the tournament stats at the top of every player screen. for the in game score board instead of Host and Client, put the player assigned number, Host, Player 1, Player 2, Player 3, Player 4, etc ...

keep track of the winners, any time someone looses they are out of playing another game until all players have played and only one have won all matches, that is when a round will end, and we should display on all players screens (not just the host) the end round stats of wins and loses.

if only two players are playing, bypass all the turnament setup and drop them into a game where they can play eachother.

for 3 players
two players pair off, one spectates
say host and player 1 play, player 2 spectates.
host wins and the new game button starts a new game with player 2 and Host (host plays opposite type x or o)
whoever wins wins the game and new game resets and selects two random new players (Lets keep global scores for each player until the host switches games keep a running stats on how many games each player wins or looses for showing between game sets, but this total is different from the game score within a set)

if there are 4 players
2 games starts
for example Host and player 2 play together and Player 1 and player 3 play together
pick a leader for the player 1 and player 3 game that person is the mini-host they will have the new game button
When one of the two games finishes, say host and player 2, host wins, when they click new game and the other game isn't finished it'll cause them to spectate, the other game of player 1 and 3. when that game finishes and say player 1 wins, the new game button for the mini-host will cause Host and player 1 to start their game. the winner of that game, say host will win the set! display the total games won/loses for all players, new game will then spawn two new games of random players.

with 5 players like 4, but add the spectator into the rotation. continue trend for 5+

=== [2025-11-21] simple-games ===
The player rotation is still broken.
spectator never gets a turn, play mostly flips between the two original players, swapping x and o. but sometimes they both get it and can't move.

Lets have it this way for both connect 4 and tic-tac-toe

for auto assign
pick random groups of 2 players and have them battle.
if there is an odd number of players as soon as one of the games resolve have them play the winner

keep track of the winners, any time someone looses they are out of playing another game until all players have played and only one have one all matches.

example 3 players
two players pair off, one spectates
say host and player 1 play, player 2 spectates.
host wins and the new game button starts a new game with player 2 and Host (host plays opposite type x or o)
whoever wins wins the game and new game resets and selects two random new players (Lets keep global scores for each player until the host switches games keep a running stats on how many games each player wins or looses for showing between game sets, but this total is different from the game score within a set)

if there are 4 players
2 games starts
for example Host and player 2 play together and Player 1 and player 3 play together
pick a leader for the player 1 and player 3 game that person is the mini-host they will have the new game button
When one of the two games finishes, say host and player 2, host wins, when they click new game and the other game isn't finished it'll cause them to spectate, the other game of player 1 and 3. when that game finishes and say player 1 wins, the new game button for the mini-host will cause Host and player 1 to start their game. the winner of that game, say host will win the set! display the total games won/loses for all players, new game will then spawn two new games of random players.

two players pair off, one spectates

host wins and the new game button starts a new game with player 2 and Host (host plays opposite type x or o)

2 games starts

with 5 players like 4, but add the spectator into the rotation. continue trend for 5+

This error happens if you call setState() on a State object for a widget that no longer appears in the widget tree (e.g., whose parent widget no longer includes the widget in its build). This error can occur when code calls setState() from a timer or an animation callback.

=== [2025-12-02] homeschool-keeper ===
Lets create some markdown files to help us plan this new app! (no code yet)

I wrote this description:
An app/site to plan, task, and journal student home school logs to keep with record laws of the various states, ease the burdens of parents to help task out and daily plan for their students education. Offering a parent, and student logins.

for the backend I want a go service, mongodb, for mobile I'm wanting flutter, for the front end I'm thinking vue3/typescript or Flutter. (how well does the web target of flutter work? would I be better making that in vue3?)

as for the app itself:
I need a way of helping me and my wife better keep track of our kids education and course work hours. I need to be able to save pictures and documents of their work. record the number of hours they spend on various subjects (core subjects and electives) I need to have the ability to create a family/organization, those organizations will have admins (the mom/dad or others) and students (the kids)

phase 1: we need to keep records of each student in core and elective topics. Have a way to create an account, and add kids to it. add the core and elective subjects you'll be teaching that year, and then have easy ways of adding a daily log entry (with time/topic/description) for each student. this needs to be the most streamline use of the app, hour for each entry should be in easy steps to an hour. allow the user to set an account setting for fractions of an hour. like .15 or .25 or .5 steps, have a spinner or dropdown with common time selections

phase 2: easy export into various documents, excel, pdf, zip of pictures/student work

phase 3: create easy school year plan topic/description/specific core or elective category (subject)/students/hours needed then from those plans create daily / weekly plans for each kids or a group of kids.

for log entries we need off the cuff logging, like if my kid goes jugging for half an hour I need something to mark that easily in the app even though it wasn't in the plans or the daily todo list.

example of a plan to log entry
topic is Story of the world (SOTW) this curriculum is for the core subject of history

phase 4: logging and reporting. allow easy reports for each student, with the ability to drill down to each subject/topic and the hours they currently have and the hours still needed to meet laws.

for the student portal I was thinking the student would be able to login to the app, and fill out log entries for themselves, that would then show up for the parent/admin to mark as valid to be counted in their education journal.

I live in the state of Missouri and here's an example of the laws we have to follow for homeschooling : https://hslda.org/legal/missouri

I think having an stand alone app that can do all of those things off line would be excellent, and then have a feature where they could pay monthly/yearly to have the account sync with my cloud and allow other parents and students to work on a single family group or ogranization.

we're also dealing with student data, so encryption and account protection laws apply here. ( the Family Educational Rights & Privacy Act (FERPA), the Children’s Online Privacy Protection Act (COPPA), and the Children’s Internet Protection )

you have a short response window, please keep your responses to 2000 tokens as we flush out these plans

from AI chat:

Done! I've created 04_tool-improvements.md with the research findings.

Key Findings from Research
For Semantic Search in Go:
Best Option for Us: sqlite-vec

Same SQLite stack we already use
Handles our corpus size easily (~30k verses + talks)
No external infrastructure needed
Can upgrade later if needed
Alternative: kelindar/search - pure Go library that can generate embeddings locally with llama.cpp, but more complex.

For Vector Databases (if we scale):
Qdrant (Rust) - lightweight, fast, has Go client
Weaviate (Go!) - full-featured, built-in vectorization
Milvus - most mature but complex
For Hebrew/Greek:
openscriptures/strongs on GitHub - public domain Strong's data
Complete Study Bible API - full Strong's + lexicons via REST
Could download and index locally in SQLite
For Cross-References:
scriptures.byu.edu exists and is excellent
We could scrape it or build our own from our footnote data
My recommendation: Start with semantic search using sqlite-vec + OpenAI embeddings. It would transform our study by letting us search for concepts instead of just keywords. Want to spec that out in more detail?

I've been thning about the game to make and I'd like to do a simplified space bridge simulator, but byte sized.

We'll call it Shields Down!

He's a quick premis.
1. Enhanced tap wars - Real time space battles.
2. you have simplified consoles:
a. helm (evasive manuvers)
b. tatical (targeting and firing weapons)
c. engineering (damage repair)

but the enimies are all AI/automated and come in waves. at you

=== [2025-10-25] mobile-games ===
1. I'd like the game to be playable with just one person, so we'll need simplified consoles for 1 or 2 players, if there are more then 3 players joined then we have multiple ships that can fight to gether or against eachother, so need simple team making.
2.
a. helm: I love that swipe to dodge action, i think there should be 2 or three long dodge buttons that when a warning animation is played on the screen they have to swipe one of the dodge bars to dodge it. then there are different manuvers to tap to get closer or farther from enimies.
b. tactical: There should be a scrollable (swipable) list of targets, that can be selected, and then sub targets, engines, weapons, engines to further target down. Then various weapons (phasers/torpedos) with cooldowns, shots hit or miss, and damage is counted
c. all systems can break, a broken system must be repaired to use. if the system is helm or tactical or egineering, then those phonse screen consoles go into repair mode and that player then has to do taps and other actions to "repair" their own system. or wait for the engineer to "fix" it for them.
3. ships have shields and hull points (HP) when HP reaches 0 it's game over. 2 game modes, endless waves or comlete 10 waves for highest score. quick kills get higher points.

4. I think having just one enemy type to start with is alright, we can add more later
5. telegraphed attacks, so the helm can dodge
6. No view screen it's just buttons and indicators to enable reactive game play, maybe one day we'll add a view screen, keep that an option for a spare phone/device
7. both, host creates room, that's mdns or something on local net for others to join.
8 save high scores locally, but maybe we can have a server to connect phones over the internet and have high scores posted there. (future plans)

9. phase 1 should be simple consols and limit 3 players (no more or less) just to get mcp working, 1 ship type slow/strong
10. minimal 8bit/16bit art style for consoles, I'd like it sci-fi space (star trek LCARS) like

=== [2025-10-25] mobile-games ===
decisions:
Lets use webSockets to communicate back and forth, and lets use JSON for the data, I like that it's debuggable and human readable.

We should always try to use the newest frameworks and versions

As for state mangement, there wont be any save game or resume for now, so just raw objects that live on the host device. I'm not sure what to do about web_socket_channel? but mDNS makes sense, unless web sockets have a way of connecting to other clients on the same network that I'm unaware of?

for the repair minigames, I think that should be a new screen that over lays (hides) the main controles. it should be a serries of buttons that say tap, or swipe, and when tapped they disappear. Could label it repair sequence, or restart sequence. add a number of steps such that it'll take between 15 and 30 seconds to complete. if they are taking a long time to complete remove steps on the end so that they aren't caught up repairing the whole time. there's no failure, just tap what comes up on screen. once the sequence is complete repairs are made and the system works again.

for the engineering console it has the same minigame for itself, but to repair the other systems it's just a matter of tapping that repair button and a 10 second cooldown and the system is repaired.

When ever there is damage against the ship a system should take 1 damage point. If the system was targeted, it takes 2x damage, each system has a total of 10 health Points. systems can be repaired if they have any damage, but has the same 10 second cooldown whether it's 0/10 or 9/10 health.

ranged phaser damage should roll off exponetially, 1u should be 100% damage 2u should be 50%, 4u should be 25% and 8u should be 12% any farther no dammage taken
torpedos have a range of 16u with full damage if they travel more then 16u they detonate and anything within 1u takes full damage 2u takes 50% no damage at 3u

phasers are better against shields then torpedos and torpedos are better against hulls. 2 to 1 ratio in either direction.

I think phasers full damage does 10 shield points and 5 hull points
torpedos do 10 hull points and 5 shield points.

each ship will have it's own regen rate for shields, 1 sp per 5 seconds seems right? but lets adjust that in play testing

hulls cannot regen in play, maybe when we do single player campange we can have FLT style reloading and hull repair.

phaser should have a 5 second cool down between banks and torpedos should be 10 seconds.

I think there's a mixup in understand for dynamics between two ships

Example Scenarios:

You: CLOSE -3, Enemy: Aggressive (advances +2) → Combined -5, range decreases by 5u
You: BACK +2, Enemy: Defensive (retreats -2) → Combined 0, range stays the same
You: MAINTAIN 0, Enemy: Balanced (+1) → Combined +1, range increases by 1u

2nd line I think if you pull back +2 rane and the enemy retreats (+2 range) then you'd be 4u further aparts.

=== [2025-07-27] interactive-class ===
Let's build an app to use with as a teacher in a class setting in church sunday school (let's generalize it for more then just religious purposes).

We'll use Go as the backend, I'm not sure what to use for the DB, maybe postgres or mongodb, And Vue3 as the front end.

The app shouldn't need a login as a student, but should keep track or user state (maybe local storage based on a UUID or device id?)

The teacher can login and create a class session  with shareable qr code or short code to use on the side that'll allow a student to access the class sesson and participate digitally in the class. (the share code should only be 5 characters and not have any hard to mistake characters so no 1 I or I, no 3 or E, no 7 or F. should be numbers and a few letters)

Defining terms:
Class is generally the same group of people week to week, and a sesson is one instance of that class on a given day.

A teacher can post a poll to the class amd get real time results.

A teacher can post a question to the class and get real time results. Questions can be multiple choice or free response.

A laptop connected to a TV or projector can display a dashboard of poll and question with real-time updates and results in graphs.

A students can input a name for themselves amd can login if wished to save responses for later lookup

A students responses are anonymous by default but per question can be override to show their name.

A teacher can post questions to the class with a timer attached for discussion. The clash dashboard will have a timer with live countdown, controllable from the teacher class page. Timer can be paused. Dashboard can display free responses from classmates during the time period.

A teacher can setup an outline and schedule for the class.

A teacher can share questions, notes, and reading assignments before a class starts.

Students can see notes for classes they are apart of.

A teacher can teach multiple classes. With different students in each.

A teacher creates a class, and then can create sessons (tied to a specific date, if needed) under that class. Students when joining a session will automatically join the parent class and can see past and any future class sessons.

A student can also join a class directly with a class code.

And a student can remove themselves from a class.

A teacher can create break out sessons and assign different questions or polls to each.

Joining a break out sesson should be easy. Maybe by ID?

Have the ability for a teacher to enable breakouts, and real-time show a listing of break outs and who's in it to enable quick joining.

Allow merging of breakouts if multiple are created at the same time by students.

Also allow a teacher to manually move students between breakouts.

Allow a student to leave the breakout view to see whole class notes and as well as re-enter breakout view.

lets have the real time be enable through communication through the backend server using something like websockets?

make running locally for debugging and test easy right in VS code on whatever platform I'm working on (windows/linux) docker is fun to use to help make that happen or other like technology stacks.

=== [2025-10-07] astrotreks ===
Okay lets create some documents like copilot instructions and such.

Here's some more details on what I'm trying to accomplish with this project.

I'm looking to replicate to some extent empty epsilon or artimus bridge simmulators. Where you have a server running the game, and clients join. The clients are different parts of a ship. and there can be multiple ships in the game. I'm looking for story driven game play with the crew has to work together using these clients to fly ship. There can be multiple crews and multiple ships. We'll also need AI like parts like other ships, enemy and allies, space stations and characters that the crew can interact with on these other ships and stations. I want clients to be just about anything, laptops, tablets, browsers. I really want embedded projects like ESP32/arduinos to be able to connect as clients for physical control surfaces and interfaces. LIke physics phaser and torpedo buttons.

I imagine the clients to look and feel very sci-fi star trek LCARS like Enterprise D or E.

We'll also need some kind of scripting language the packend supports for mission files. I'm not a huge fan of Lua so maybe something else?

ask me other qustions to help better define this project.

=== [2025-10-02] forkirk ===
Note: I'm on powershell

Lets work on making quote group more versatile, I think quote groups should be able to link quotes across videos, not just from a single video.

When I had QuoteGroups in mind originally is that it would contain links to quotes objects. so you could group them together under a common theme. Instead we have a single video that we can pull quotes from.

=== [2025-10-02] forkirk ===
1. I think if a quote group is approved then all the quotes inside will also be approved (though if any are edited it goes unapproved), Though I don't want all of the individual quotes in a qoute group to also be published outside of the quote group too....
2. Lets notify the user that it's apart of a quote group (also mark on the individual quote is in a group too) and note to the user it'll also update the quote group, give them the option to clone the current qoute or update the quote in the group
3. Since there are no longer tied to one video, being able to manually sort (dragging) clips around makes the mose sense
4. Only one owner of a group
5. All three, Lets have a global default in user settings, followed by per group setting, followed by hiding individual quotes. One may want a quote in a group but it's good enough to stand on it's own.
6. We should have REST endpoints for Group quote management, but I am unsure what you mean by membership

extras
a. quoteID and videoID fields make sense to me.
b. We should have a group metadata. allow description, cover image, and tags. images should be an internet URL
c. batch actions would be very nice. lets have them
d. We need tag filtering, especially on the front home page.

Break this down into phases and make a markdown document of TODOs to track our progress
